55|f35525|    private func closeTab(_ tab: Tab) {

57|dc033d|            tabs.remove(at: index)

60|7fb881|            if activeTabId == tab.id {

63|fdd0e2|                } else {

65|51dd50|                    let newIndex = min(index, tabs.count - 1)

685|9d97c0|        .onChange(of: tab.id) { _ in
686|ba85f8|            text = tab.content
687|8e600f|            // Folding detection removed
688|5f3077|        }

691|5f3077|        }
692|588fd8|        .onChange(of: currentColumn) { col in
693|16524d|            editorCore.cursorPosition = CursorPosition(line: currentLineNumber, column: col)
694|5f3077|        }
695|75807d|        .onChange(of: editorCore.editorFontSize) { newSize in
696|494152|            // Update lineHeight to match Runestone's line height (~1.4x font size)
697|4f8334|            lineHeight = ceil(newSize * 1.4)
698|5f3077|        }
699|f5c549|        .onChange(of: editorCore.requestedGoToLine) { line in
700|5c18ef|            if let line = line {
701|304480|                requestedLineSelection = line - 1  // Convert 1-indexed to 0-indexed
702|4dd57b|                editorCore.requestedGoToLine = nil  // Clear the request
703|a7dc16|            }
704|5f3077|        }
705|2bd24e|        .onAppear {

709|5f3077|        }

720|5b2177|    let scrollOffset: CGFloat

747|27e597|    }
748|adc83b|
749|46d3db|    private func displayText(for lineIndex: Int) -> String {
750|5d97cf|        switch lineNumbersStyle {
751|a6eb36|        case "relative":
752|b0622f|            let lineNumber = lineIndex + 1
753|44bb33|            if lineNumber == currentLine { return "\(lineNumber)" }
754|5e67df|            return "\(abs(lineNumber - currentLine))"
755|adc83b|
756|5040ac|        case "interval":
757|b0622f|            let lineNumber = lineIndex + 1
758|bc3fe3|            return (lineNumber == 1 || lineNumber % 5 == 0) ? "\(lineNumber)" : ""
759|adc83b|
760|520b7d|        default:
761|3880c0|            return "\(lineIndex + 1)"
762|5f3077|        }
763|27e597|    }

124|e053f1|    private func diffIndicatorsLayer(minimapHeight: CGFloat, lineCount: Int) -> some View {
125|df88d3|        // VS Code minimap diff markers are thin and pinned to the left.
126|352402|        let barWidth: CGFloat = 2
127|adc83b|
128|eb7497|        // Guard against division by zero
129|dad1b1|        if lineCount > 0 {
130|82ebe9|            ForEach(diffIndicators) { indicator in
131|c4c9a2|                let startLine = max(0, min(indicator.lineRange.lowerBound, lineCount - 1))
132|d34bb2|                let endLineExclusive = max(startLine + 1, min(indicator.lineRange.upperBound, lineCount))
133|adc83b|
134|7e47a5|                let startY = (CGFloat(startLine) / CGFloat(max(lineCount, 1))) * minimapHeight
135|634593|                let endY = (CGFloat(endLineExclusive) / CGFloat(max(lineCount, 1))) * minimapHeight
136|13ec78|                let height = max(2, endY - startY)
137|adc83b|
138|ff13e9|                Rectangle()
139|41dcad|                    .fill(diffColor(for: indicator.kind).opacity(0.95))
140|81c659|                    .frame(width: barWidth, height: height)
141|72358e|                    .offset(x: 0, y: startY)

143|5f3077|        }

146|906d12|    // MARK: - Visible region math
147|adc83b|
148|6919f3|    private func visibleRegionHeight(minimapHeight: CGFloat) -> CGFloat {
149|ff17e8|        guard totalContentHeight > 0 else { return 0 }
150|c5f520|        let ratio = scrollViewHeight / totalContentHeight
151|f9bc55|        return minimapHeight * min(max(ratio, 0), 1.0)
152|27e597|    }
153|adc83b|
154|ee5041|    private func visibleRegionOffset(minimapHeight: CGFloat, visibleHeight: CGFloat) -> CGFloat {
155|7da55c|        let scrollable = max(0, totalContentHeight - scrollViewHeight)
156|45fee0|        guard scrollable > 0 else { return 0 }
157|adc83b|
158|e13930|        let scrollRatio = min(max(scrollOffset / scrollable, 0), 1.0)
159|7c51ab|        return scrollRatio * max(0, minimapHeight - visibleHeight)
160|27e597|    }

162|04759d|    // MARK: - Interaction
163|adc83b|
164|7ef7ff|    /// Requests scroll so that the main editor's visible region is centered around the minimap Y position.
165|783b1d|    /// Uses callback to parent - minimap never directly controls editor scroll (prevents jitter).
166|92b230|    private func updateScroll(forMinimapY yPosition: CGFloat, minimapHeight: CGFloat) {
167|78fab1|        guard totalContentHeight > 0 else { return }
168|dac0ba|        guard let onScrollRequested = onScrollRequested else { return }
169|adc83b|
170|783533|        let clampedY = max(0, min(yPosition, minimapHeight))
171|89fa92|        let ratio = (minimapHeight > 0) ? (clampedY / minimapHeight) : 0
172|adc83b|
173|e4e280|        // Target a center position (VS Code behavior).
174|3b7590|        let targetCenter = ratio * totalContentHeight
175|b9ce99|        let desiredOffset = targetCenter - (scrollViewHeight / 2)
176|adc83b|
177|5b5c2d|        let maxOffset = max(0, totalContentHeight - scrollViewHeight)
178|6a7c82|        let newOffset = min(max(desiredOffset, 0), maxOffset)
179|d6ed84|        
180|73b1e7|        // Request scroll via callback - parent controls the actual scroll
181|f186d0|        onScrollRequested(newOffset)
182|27e597|    }

184|57db31|    // MARK: - Rendering (Canvas)
185|adc83b|
186|ddfd07|    private func drawMinimapPreview(
187|1dbb0f|        in context: inout GraphicsContext,
188|8ae978|        size: CGSize,
189|e54bca|        lines: [Substring]
190|981e04|    ) {
191|c96a6f|        let paddingX: CGFloat = 4
192|435081|        let paddingY: CGFloat = 2
193|adc83b|
194|c711e9|        let contentWidth = max(0, size.width - (paddingX * 2))
195|6c41d9|        let contentHeight = max(0, size.height - (paddingY * 2))
196|adc83b|
197|82f19e|        guard contentWidth > 0, contentHeight > 0 else { return }
198|adc83b|
199|ad5ba7|        let lineCount = max(lines.count, 1)
200|d6ed84|        
201|02e15c|        // FIXED: Use fixed pixels per line (VS Code style) instead of stretching to fill
202|54f182|        // This ensures the minimap always shows a tiny preview regardless of file size
203|3065bb|        let targetPixelsPerLine: CGFloat = 2.5
204|7dd91a|        let pixelsPerLine = targetPixelsPerLine
205|d6ed84|        
206|9b2a64|        // Calculate how many lines we can show in the minimap
207|3e694e|        let visibleLines = Int(contentHeight / pixelsPerLine)
208|d6ed84|        
209|1d6fd4|        // Calculate scroll offset to show the right portion of the document
210|91f804|        // Use scrollOffset and totalContentHeight to calculate current position
211|738fb2|        let scrollRatio = totalContentHeight > 0 ? Double(scrollOffset) / Double(max(totalContentHeight - scrollViewHeight, 1)) : 0
212|5d3dc8|        let startLine = max(0, Int(scrollRatio * Double(max(0, lineCount - visibleLines))))
213|adc83b|
214|03dc30|        // Token-block mode (colored rectangles) - VS Code style minimap
215|200364|        let minBarHeight: CGFloat = 1
216|f6b381|        let barHeight = max(minBarHeight, pixelsPerLine)
217|adc83b|
218|d1e35f|        // Approximate "characters" across minimap width.
219|26fc02|        let maxChars: CGFloat = 120
220|64e37a|        let charWidth = contentWidth / maxChars
221|adc83b|
222|dd472a|        // Render lines starting from startLine (scrolls with document)
223|8082c0|        let endLine = min(startLine + visibleLines + 1, lineCount)
224|d6ed84|        
225|5be8fa|        // Guard against invalid range (endLine must be >= startLine)
226|4957c8|        guard endLine >= startLine else { return }
227|d6ed84|        
228|714e33|        for i in startLine..<endLine {
229|794e26|            let displayIndex = i - startLine
230|82adeb|            let y = paddingY + (CGFloat(displayIndex) * pixelsPerLine)
231|db9e6f|            if y > size.height { break }
232|adc83b|
233|87a58d|            let line = lines.indices.contains(i) ? lines[i] : Substring("")
234|1922e4|            let tokens = tokenize(line)
235|adc83b|
236|ed9464|            var x = paddingX
237|4f7785|            let yAligned = y.rounded(FloatingPointRoundingRule.down)
238|adc83b|
239|993665|            if tokens.isEmpty {
240|e53354|                // Render faint whitespace line.
241|852310|                let rect = CGRect(x: x, y: yAligned, width: max(4, contentWidth * 0.15), height: barHeight)
242|afc890|                context.fill(Path(rect), with: .color(Color(white: 0.45).opacity(0.10)))
243|1df510|                continue
244|a7dc16|            }
245|adc83b|
246|3f8f53|            for token in tokens {
247|0ef518|                guard x < (paddingX + contentWidth) else { break }
248|6f9f42|                let w = max(1, CGFloat(token.text.count) * charWidth)
249|4a0a54|                let rect = CGRect(x: x, y: yAligned, width: min(w, paddingX + contentWidth - x), height: barHeight)
250|0a74f9|                context.fill(Path(rect), with: .color(token.color.opacity(0.80)))
251|354777|                x += w
252|a7dc16|            }
253|5f3077|        }
254|27e597|    }
255|adc83b|
256|3b9c43|    // MARK: - Syntax highlighting (lightweight)
257|adc83b|
258|342387|    private struct Token {
259|2ac01d|        enum Kind {
260|566b1c|            case plain
261|5d29ef|            case keyword
262|0603c2|            case string
263|d9fad7|            case comment
264|efbbfd|            case number
265|6e9645|            case typeName
266|5f3077|        }
267|adc83b|
268|f051aa|        var text: Substring
269|f8a374|        var kind: Kind
270|adc83b|
271|b98be5|        var color: Color {
272|157398|            switch kind {
273|706e3d|            case .plain:
274|7f1b9e|                return Color(white: 0.70)
275|b19882|            case .keyword:
276|5f4852|                return Color(red: 0.78, green: 0.53, blue: 0.95) // purple-ish
277|b4c397|            case .string:
278|964852|                return Color(red: 0.80, green: 0.72, blue: 0.43) // yellow-ish
279|3ded9b|            case .comment:
280|37e86a|                return Color(red: 0.46, green: 0.60, blue: 0.50) // green-ish
281|fea990|            case .number:
282|c38f5f|                return Color(red: 0.40, green: 0.73, blue: 0.92) // blue-ish
283|2c017e|            case .typeName:
284|5585ef|                return Color(red: 0.45, green: 0.83, blue: 0.70) // teal-ish
285|a7dc16|            }
286|5f3077|        }
287|27e597|    }
288|adc83b|
289|10bee9|    private func makeAttributedLine(from line: Substring, fontSize: CGFloat) -> AttributedString {
290|a59ad5|        let tokens = tokenize(line)
291|adc83b|
292|1b63ae|        var out = AttributedString()
293|09ef1f|        for token in tokens {
294|d1233d|            var chunk = AttributedString(String(token.text))
295|9befb1|            chunk.font = .system(size: fontSize, weight: .regular, design: .monospaced)
296|97f23a|            chunk.foregroundColor = token.color
297|af1a00|            out.append(chunk)
298|5f3077|        }
299|adc83b|
300|d11742|        if out.characters.isEmpty {
301|e5b85c|            // Preserve a tiny amount of "whitespace presence" so empty lines still show.
302|9dd08f|            var chunk = AttributedString(" ")
303|9befb1|            chunk.font = .system(size: fontSize, weight: .regular, design: .monospaced)
304|8cb2a3|            chunk.foregroundColor = Color(white: 0.7).opacity(0.25)
305|af1a00|            out.append(chunk)
306|5f3077|        }
307|adc83b|
308|9231ab|        return out
309|27e597|    }
310|adc83b|
311|4abcd7|    private func tokenize(_ line: Substring) -> [Token] {
312|f0a25f|        // Extremely lightweight tokenizer:
313|6188fb|        // - full-line comment if first non-space is # (python-like)
314|de2ec8|        // - inline comment starting at //
315|0a0697|        // - strings in "..." or '...'
316|efb1f5|        // - numbers
317|23cdc0|        // - keywords
318|43ec2e|        // - PascalCase tokens treated as type names
319|39dd2a|        var tokens: [Token] = []
320|3d99ce|        var i = line.startIndex
321|adc83b|
322|600872|        func peek(_ offset: Int = 0) -> Character? {
323|34ecda|            var idx = i
324|c6ee90|            for _ in 0..<offset {
325|2838dc|                guard idx < line.endIndex else { return nil }
326|306cea|                idx = line.index(after: idx)
327|a7dc16|            }
328|5bdcc9|            return idx < line.endIndex ? line[idx] : nil
329|5f3077|        }
330|adc83b|
331|5ea689|        func advance(_ n: Int = 1) {
332|293115|            for _ in 0..<n {
333|42c484|                guard i < line.endIndex else { return }
334|10bf0b|                i = line.index(after: i)
335|a7dc16|            }
336|5f3077|        }
337|adc83b|
338|80ae1a|        // Detect python/shebang-like comment lines: first non-whitespace is '#'
339|5015b2|        if let firstNonSpace = line.firstIndex(where: { !$0.isWhitespace }),
340|fc3e36|           line[firstNonSpace] == "#" {
341|a7cd18|            tokens.append(Token(text: line[line.startIndex..<line.endIndex], kind: .comment))
342|41c689|            return tokens
343|5f3077|        }
344|adc83b|
345|544fab|        while i < line.endIndex {
346|7e4e40|            let ch = line[i]
347|adc83b|
348|40eeea|            // Inline comment: //
349|8fbe15|            if ch == "/", peek(1) == "/" {
350|860932|                let range = i..<line.endIndex
351|b67a6a|                tokens.append(Token(text: line[range], kind: .comment))
352|23d68f|                return tokens
353|a7dc16|            }
354|adc83b|
355|41a694|            // Whitespace
356|76957e|            if ch.isWhitespace {
357|eae3bb|                let start = i
358|7f4f8a|                while i < line.endIndex, line[i].isWhitespace { advance() }
359|3f1e7d|                tokens.append(Token(text: line[start..<i], kind: .plain))
360|1df510|                continue
361|a7dc16|            }
362|adc83b|
363|e53ff2|            // String literals
364|899c9c|            if ch == "\"" || ch == "'" {
365|9d8090|                let quote = ch
366|eae3bb|                let start = i
367|e2aa2f|                advance()
368|4ed8ff|                var escaped = false
369|3876db|                while i < line.endIndex {
370|9c755e|                    let c = line[i]
371|605f4e|                    if escaped {
372|cb9c8a|                        escaped = false
373|3f9321|                        advance()
374|e47242|                        continue
375|c9717a|                    }
376|7f8424|                    if c == "\\" {
377|37863a|                        escaped = true
378|3f9321|                        advance()
379|e47242|                        continue
380|c9717a|                    }
381|d1886f|                    if c == quote {
382|3f9321|                        advance()
383|28a64b|                        break
384|c9717a|                    }
385|7c96dd|                    advance()
386|4e2d32|                }
387|9305c9|                tokens.append(Token(text: line[start..<i], kind: .string))
388|1df510|                continue
389|a7dc16|            }
390|adc83b|
391|bd52f1|            // Numbers
392|38cd36|            if ch.isNumber {
393|eae3bb|                let start = i
394|89de1b|                while i < line.endIndex, line[i].isNumber || line[i] == "." { advance() }
395|8480cb|                tokens.append(Token(text: line[start..<i], kind: .number))
396|1df510|                continue
397|a7dc16|            }
398|adc83b|
399|1b4cce|            // Identifiers / keywords
400|181e74|            if ch.isLetter || ch == "_" {
401|eae3bb|                let start = i
402|e2aa2f|                advance()
403|3876db|                while i < line.endIndex {
404|9c755e|                    let c = line[i]
405|e225c5|                    if c.isLetter || c.isNumber || c == "_" { advance() } else { break }
406|4e2d32|                }
407|cd95c9|                let word = line[start..<i]
408|8aa092|                let kind: Token.Kind
409|adc83b|
410|08878f|                if isKeyword(word) {
411|74c41d|                    kind = .keyword
412|be7b6b|                } else if looksLikeTypeName(word) {
413|00ef8c|                    kind = .typeName
414|fdd0e2|                } else {
415|d46347|                    kind = .plain
416|4e2d32|                }
417|adc83b|
418|d43ef3|                tokens.append(Token(text: word, kind: kind))
419|1df510|                continue
420|a7dc16|            }
421|adc83b|
422|612c55|            // Operators / punctuation
423|953483|            let start = i
424|acf00b|            advance()
425|f768b8|            tokens.append(Token(text: line[start..<i], kind: .plain))
426|5f3077|        }
427|adc83b|
428|50a443|        return tokens
429|27e597|    }
430|adc83b|
431|3facb7|    private func isKeyword(_ word: Substring) -> Bool {
432|c4f25e|        // Small superset of common Swift/JS/Python keywords.
433|b2b9d9|        // (We can't depend on a full parser here.)
434|396c95|        let keywords: Set<String> = [
435|9af6d0|            "import", "export", "from", "as",
436|dbd304|            "struct", "class", "enum", "protocol", "extension", "func", "var", "let",
437|bd4ed1|            "if", "else", "for", "while", "repeat", "switch", "case", "default",
438|e351bd|            "break", "continue", "return", "throw", "throws", "try", "catch",
439|b9f132|            "do", "in", "where", "guard", "defer",
440|511559|            "public", "private", "fileprivate", "internal", "open",
441|12dd92|            "static", "final", "override", "mutating", "nonmutating",
442|91d838|            "async", "await",
443|6f6f8c|            "true", "false", "nil",
444|0cf8cf|            "self", "super",
445|e39cc4|            // JS/Python-ish
446|ad9513|            "const", "function", "async", "await", "new", "this",
447|1c9b9e|            "def", "pass", "lambda", "None"
448|220505|        ]
449|0da584|        return keywords.contains(String(word))
450|27e597|    }
451|adc83b|
452|e0492d|    private func looksLikeTypeName(_ word: Substring) -> Bool {
453|ce64a9|        // Simple heuristic: PascalCase (leading uppercase).
454|bbf2da|        guard let first = word.first else { return false }
455|248546|        return first.isUppercase
456|27e597|    }
457|adc83b|
458|e2a5f4|    // MARK: - Diff colors
459|adc83b|
460|af35e5|    private func diffColor(for kind: MinimapDiffIndicator.Kind) -> Color {
461|01fe0f|        switch kind {
462|e91923|        case .added:
463|97b08e|            return Color.green
464|1a0dfa|        case .modified:
465|a71900|            return Color.red
466|4fc3e2|        case .deleted:
467|7296db|            // VS Code uses red-ish for deletions too; keep distinct via slightly different tone.
468|c59220|            return Color(red: 1.0, green: 0.35, blue: 0.35)
469|5f3077|        }
470|27e597|    }

124|2505dd|    @State private var sortOption: SortOption = .fileName
125|3ee770|    @State private var sortAscending: Bool = true
126|d6760e|    @State private var selectedExtensions: Set<String> = []
127|bb7bcd|    @State private var groupByDirectory: Bool = false

135|b4687f|    
136|50903b|    // Binary file extensions to exclude
137|f1d796|    private let binaryExtensions = [".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png", ".gif", ".bmp", ".ico", ".pdf", ".zip", ".tar", ".gz", ".mp3", ".mp4", ".avi", ".mov", ".exe", ".dll", ".so", ".dylib", ".app", ".ipa", ".ipa", ".dmg", ".pkg", ".deb", ".rpm", ".img", ".iso", ".bin", ".dat", ".db", ".sqlite", ".sqlite3", ".ttf", ".otf", ".woff", ".woff2", ".eot"]

146|b4687f|    
147|f96259|    /// Returns the filtered, sorted, and limited results
148|f32b09|    var processedResults: [FileSearchResult] {
149|1a5bc0|        var filtered = rawResults
150|d6ed84|        
151|0a214d|        // 1. Filter by binary files
152|99c850|        if excludeBinaryFiles {
153|9b3c53|            filtered = filtered.filter { result in
154|74a475|                let ext = (result.fileName as NSString).pathExtension.lowercased()
155|979d9d|                return !binaryExtensions.contains(where: { $0.lowercased().hasSuffix(ext) })
156|a7dc16|            }
157|5f3077|        }
158|d6ed84|        
159|23706c|        // 2. Filter by selected extensions
160|8f0448|        if !selectedExtensions.isEmpty {
161|9b3c53|            filtered = filtered.filter { result in
162|74a475|                let ext = (result.fileName as NSString).pathExtension.lowercased()
163|db0fb9|                return selectedExtensions.contains { $0.lowercased().dropFirst() == ext }
164|a7dc16|            }
165|5f3077|        }
166|d6ed84|        
167|e35546|        // 3. Sort results
168|b5c3d5|        filtered = filtered.sorted { lhs, rhs in
169|cc07ab|            switch sortOption {
170|2eb58c|            case .fileName:
171|c61e48|                return sortAscending ? lhs.fileName < rhs.fileName : lhs.fileName > rhs.fileName
172|7a14db|            case .path:
173|8db7c1|                return sortAscending ? lhs.path < rhs.path : lhs.path > rhs.path
174|f24236|            case .matches:
175|beb3b2|                return sortAscending ? lhs.matches.count < rhs.matches.count : lhs.matches.count > rhs.matches.count
176|a7dc16|            }
177|5f3077|        }
178|d6ed84|        
179|b622d3|        // 4. Apply result limit
180|2f53d7|        if let maxCount = resultLimit.maxCount, filtered.count > maxCount {
181|78a06d|            filtered = Array(filtered.prefix(maxCount))
182|5f3077|        }
183|d6ed84|        
184|ed0d9a|        return filtered
185|27e597|    }
186|b4687f|    
187|afa680|    /// Group results by directory if enabled
188|bf562e|    var groupedResults: [(key: String, results: [FileSearchResult])] {
189|cfef88|        if groupByDirectory {
190|f958d9|            let grouped = Dictionary(grouping: processedResults) { $0.directory }
191|9c37af|            return grouped.sorted { $0.key < $1.key }.map { (key: $0.key, results: $0.value) }
192|b31999|        } else {
193|01a805|            return [(key: "", results: processedResults)]
194|5f3077|        }
195|27e597|    }
196|b4687f|    
197|7eee45|    /// All unique extensions from current results
198|8335d0|    var availableExtensions: [String] {
199|f40721|        let extensions = rawResults.map { (result: FileSearchResult) -> String in
200|b157b5|            let ext = (result.fileName as NSString).pathExtension
201|5a54b3|            return ext.isEmpty ? "noext" : ext.lowercased()
202|5f3077|        }
203|69f3ad|        return Array(Set(extensions)).sorted()
204|27e597|    }
205|b4687f|    
206|12bc82|    // MARK: - Keyboard Navigation Functions
207|b4687f|    
208|f6a132|    /// Builds the flat list of navigation items from results
209|e5849c|    private func buildNavigationItems() -> [SearchNavigationItem] {
210|ccfc3e|        var items: [SearchNavigationItem] = []
211|ad57e8|        let results = processedResults
212|ce48df|        for (fileIndex, fileResult) in results.enumerated() {
213|8e1a42|            for (matchIndex, match) in fileResult.matches.enumerated() {
214|e47853|                items.append(SearchNavigationItem(
215|ef8b8c|                    fileIndex: fileIndex,
216|e7bbe5|                    matchIndex: matchIndex,
217|ef4b99|                    fileID: fileResult.id,
218|a88193|                    matchID: match.id
219|2188d8|                ))
220|a7dc16|            }
221|5f3077|        }
222|1d239a|        return items
223|27e597|    }

240|27e597|    }

255|b84c76|    /// Navigates to next result
256|639992|    private func navigateToNextResult() {
257|e554e3|        guard !navigationItems.isEmpty else { return }
258|d6ed84|        
259|82d91a|        if let current = selectedNavigationItem,
260|e6502a|           let currentIndex = navigationItems.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == current.id }) {
261|9ddba8|            let nextIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % navigationItems.count
262|59a7a6|            selectedNavigationItem = navigationItems[nextIndex]
263|b31999|        } else {
264|dec0e2|            selectedNavigationItem = navigationItems.first
265|5f3077|        }
266|27e597|    }
267|b4687f|    
268|56119f|    /// Navigates to previous result
269|8adb23|    private func navigateToPreviousResult() {
270|e554e3|        guard !navigationItems.isEmpty else { return }
271|d6ed84|        
272|82d91a|        if let current = selectedNavigationItem,
273|e6502a|           let currentIndex = navigationItems.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == current.id }) {
274|378834|            let prevIndex = (currentIndex - 1 + navigationItems.count) % navigationItems.count
275|c2bab4|            selectedNavigationItem = navigationItems[prevIndex]
276|b31999|        } else {
277|3109a0|            selectedNavigationItem = navigationItems.last
278|5f3077|        }
279|27e597|    }
280|b4687f|    
281|15b717|    /// Opens the currently selected result
282|a787fe|    private func openSelectedResult() {
283|f4616c|        guard let selected = selectedNavigationItem else { return }
284|ad57e8|        let results = processedResults
285|c8f72e|        guard selected.fileIndex < results.count else { return }
286|bdd740|        let fileResult = results[selected.fileIndex]
287|4f603d|        guard selected.matchIndex < fileResult.matches.count else { return }
288|08d2f8|        let match = fileResult.matches[selected.matchIndex]
289|e4b372|        onResultSelected?(fileResult.path, match.lineNumber)
290|27e597|    }

747|413a48|    private func setupDebouncedSearch() {
748|ba1ced|        // Note: Debounced search is handled via onChange modifier and debouncedSearch() function
749|27e597|    }
750|b4687f|    
751|101550|    // MARK: - Debounced Search
752|b4687f|    
753|6320bf|    private func debouncedSearch(immediate: Bool = false) {
754|5ed5cb|        debounceCancellable?.cancel()
755|d6ed84|        
756|26b670|        if immediate {
757|47ed6c|            performDebouncedSearch(query: searchText)
758|b31999|        } else {
759|dcccb0|            setupDebouncedSearch()
760|5f3077|        }
761|27e597|    }
762|b4687f|    
763|1d3cf0|    private func performDebouncedSearch(query: String) {
764|798fdb|        searchTask?.cancel()
765|d6ed84|        
766|e78100|        guard query.count >= 2 else { return }
767|d6ed84|        
768|86191b|        let options = SearchManager.SearchOptions(
769|212967|            isCaseSensitive: matchCase,
770|d0fada|            isWholeWord: matchWholeWord,
771|31ed2c|            isRegex: useRegex
772|3143a4|        )
773|d6ed84|        
774|bed986|        let includeGlobs = filesToInclude
775|646476|            .split(separator: ",")
776|6c985e|            .map { $0.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) }
777|c71ead|            .filter { !$0.isEmpty }
778|d6ed84|        
779|ce8d1a|        let excludeGlobs = filesToExclude
780|646476|            .split(separator: ",")
781|6c985e|            .map { $0.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) }
782|c71ead|            .filter { !$0.isEmpty }
783|d6ed84|        
784|78ed4e|        let searchQuery = SearchManager.SearchQuery(
785|5f3d5e|            text: query,
786|62f7ee|            options: options,
787|ca52d5|            includeGlobs: includeGlobs,
788|f1536d|            excludeGlobs: excludeGlobs
789|3143a4|        )
790|d6ed84|        
791|6b2788|        searchTask = Task { [weak searchManager] in
792|597ee6|            guard let manager = searchManager else { return }
793|08ebed|            guard !Task.isCancelled else { return }
794|2e2a14|            manager.search(in: rootURL, query: searchQuery)
795|5f3077|        }
796|27e597|    }

810|27e597|    }

812|eb174a|    private func performReplace() {
813|a606b5|        guard !searchText.isEmpty && !replaceText.isEmpty else { return }
814|d6ed84|        
815|86191b|        let options = SearchManager.SearchOptions(
816|212967|            isCaseSensitive: matchCase,
817|d0fada|            isWholeWord: matchWholeWord,
818|31ed2c|            isRegex: useRegex
819|3143a4|        )
820|d6ed84|        
821|bed986|        let includeGlobs = filesToInclude
822|646476|            .split(separator: ",")
823|6c985e|            .map { $0.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) }
824|c71ead|            .filter { !$0.isEmpty }
825|d6ed84|        
826|ce8d1a|        let excludeGlobs = filesToExclude
827|646476|            .split(separator: ",")
828|6c985e|            .map { $0.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) }
829|c71ead|            .filter { !$0.isEmpty }
830|d6ed84|        
831|87daa1|        let query = SearchManager.SearchQuery(
832|29db41|            text: searchText,
833|62f7ee|            options: options,
834|ca52d5|            includeGlobs: includeGlobs,
835|f1536d|            excludeGlobs: excludeGlobs
836|3143a4|        )
837|d6ed84|        
838|0f1953|        Task {
839|71cc09|            do {
840|c52263|                let result = try await searchManager.replace(in: rootURL, query: query, replacement: replaceText)
841|71387f|                print("Replace completed: \(result.replacements) replacements in \(result.filesTouched) files")
842|91b9a2|            } catch {
843|e1dc9b|                print("Replace failed: \(error.localizedDescription)")
844|a7dc16|            }
845|5f3077|        }
846|27e597|    }

1|d755ba|import SwiftUI
2|adc83b|
3|444a0a|struct StickyHeaderView: View {
4|e25e12|    let text: String
5|c75d8a|    let currentLine: Int
6|6b0e55|    let theme: Theme
7|96ac71|    let lineHeight: CGFloat
8|98f24f|    let onSelect: (Int) -> Void
9|b4687f|    
10|1c61db|    @State private var stickyLines: [(line: Int, content: String, depth: Int)] = []
11|b4687f|    
12|504e43|    var body: some View {
13|0865e6|        VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 0) {
14|64c1f0|            ForEach(stickyLines, id: \.line) { item in
15|d591fc|                HStack {
16|95a47f|                    Text(item.content.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces))
17|aa72a2|                        .font(.system(size: 14, weight: .regular, design: .monospaced))
18|49a616|                        .foregroundColor(theme.editorForeground)
19|a2fdad|                        .padding(.leading, CGFloat(item.depth) * 16 + 4)
20|30e6ec|                        .padding(.vertical, 2)
21|dcd0bf|                    Spacer()
22|4e2d32|                }
23|ebee1c|                .frame(height: lineHeight)
24|f5e36b|                .background(theme.editorBackground.opacity(0.95))
25|8fca9f|                .overlay(Rectangle().frame(height: 1).foregroundColor(theme.sidebarBackground), alignment: .bottom)
26|3c1044|                .onTapGesture {
27|edfb18|                    onSelect(item.line)
28|4e2d32|                }
29|a7dc16|            }
30|5f3077|        }
31|17b768|        .onChange(of: currentLine) { _ in updateStickyLines() }
32|3bab08|        .onAppear { updateStickyLines() }
33|27e597|    }
34|b4687f|    
35|d568aa|    private func updateStickyLines() {
36|c8d949|        // Simplified logic: scan upwards from currentLine for class/func definitions
37|8a78a4|        // In a real app, use AST or Symbol Table
38|d6ed84|        
39|2f18b4|        let lines = text.components(separatedBy: .newlines)
40|a78be9|        guard currentLine < lines.count else { return }
41|d6ed84|        
42|d055db|        var found: [(line: Int, content: String, depth: Int)] = []
43|5a8108|        var minIndent = Int.max
44|d6ed84|        
45|c529bb|        // Scan upwards
46|b90d30|        for i in stride(from: currentLine, through: 0, by: -1) {
47|ef0328|            let line = lines[i]
48|ec6750|            let trimmed = line.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces)
49|3070d1|            
50|f62167|            if trimmed.isEmpty || trimmed.hasPrefix("//") { continue }
51|3070d1|            
52|048a4f|            let indent = line.prefix(while: { $0 == " " }).count / 4
53|3070d1|            
54|f38ce9|            // Heuristic: declarations usually have less indentation than current scope
55|b74045|            // and contain keywords
56|8bf583|            if indent < minIndent {
57|bbf15e|                if trimmed.hasPrefix("class ") || 
58|8e0f1d|                   trimmed.hasPrefix("struct ") || 
59|234574|                   trimmed.hasPrefix("enum ") || 
60|f5082c|                   trimmed.hasPrefix("func ") || 
61|06a1ce|                   trimmed.hasPrefix("extension ") ||
62|c9379e|                   trimmed.contains(" body: some View") {
63|dd2193|                    
64|4c83b4|                    found.insert((i, line, indent), at: 0)
65|652b6b|                    minIndent = indent
66|4e2d32|                }
67|a7dc16|            }
68|3070d1|            
69|718c12|            if minIndent == 0 { break }
70|5f3077|        }
71|d6ed84|        
72|4c5bf2|        // Limit to 3 levels to avoid clutter
73|b8bbaf|        if found.count > 3 {
74|60ca6d|            found = Array(found.suffix(3))
75|5f3077|        }
76|d6ed84|        
77|7355d8|        self.stickyLines = found
78|27e597|    }
79|b31277|}

52|048a4f|            let indent = line.prefix(while: { $0 == " " }).count / 4
53|3070d1|            
54|f38ce9|            // Heuristic: declarations usually have less indentation than current scope
55|b74045|            // and contain keywords
56|8bf583|            if indent < minIndent {
57|bbf15e|                if trimmed.hasPrefix("class ") || 
58|8e0f1d|                   trimmed.hasPrefix("struct ") || 
59|234574|                   trimmed.hasPrefix("enum ") || 
60|f5082c|                   trimmed.hasPrefix("func ") || 
61|06a1ce|                   trimmed.hasPrefix("extension ") ||
62|c9379e|                   trimmed.contains(" body: some View") {
63|dd2193|                    
64|4c83b4|                    found.insert((i, line, indent), at: 0)
65|652b6b|                    minIndent = indent
66|4e2d32|                }
67|a7dc16|            }
68|3070d1|            
69|718c12|            if minIndent == 0 { break }
70|5f3077|        }
71|d6ed84|        
72|4c5bf2|        // Limit to 3 levels to avoid clutter
73|b8bbaf|        if found.count > 3 {
74|60ca6d|            found = Array(found.suffix(3))
75|5f3077|        }
76|d6ed84|        
77|7355d8|        self.stickyLines = found
78|27e597|    }
79|b31277|}

425|fb5c90|class TerminalWorkspace: ObservableObject {
426|bef14f|    static let shared = TerminalWorkspace()
427|adc83b|
428|65ba2d|    @Published var tabs: [TerminalTab] = []
429|e129c3|    @Published var activeTabId: UUID?
430|adc83b|
431|75cc04|    var activeTabIndex: Int? {
432|1af0c1|        guard let id = activeTabId else { return nil }
433|461110|        return tabs.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == id })
434|27e597|    }
435|adc83b|

438|3fc8ba|        return tabs[idx]

441|2a046a|    var activePane: TerminalManager? {

450|ff5787|    func addTab() {
451|d110cf|        let term = TerminalManager()
452|79d501|        term.title = "Terminal \(tabs.count + 1)"
453|208e89|        let tab = TerminalTab(panes: [term])
454|a630ed|        tabs.append(tab)
455|4370c7|        activeTabId = tab.id
456|27e597|    }
457|adc83b|
458|32d0a2|    func closeTab(id: UUID) {
459|a1d7f5|        guard let idx = tabs.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == id }) else { return }
460|dbcf27|        for pane in tabs[idx].panes {
461|dd970f|            pane.disconnect()
462|5f3077|        }
463|bf3ad9|        tabs.remove(at: idx)
464|7a2997|        if activeTabId == id {
465|04b8bb|            activeTabId = tabs.last?.id
466|5f3077|        }
467|27e597|    }
468|adc83b|
469|7f1ee2|    func setActivePane(_ paneId: UUID, in tabId: UUID) {
470|82eb46|        guard let tabIndex = tabs.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == tabId }) else { return }
471|9992f8|        tabs[tabIndex].activePaneId = paneId
472|27e597|    }
473|adc83b|
474|1ed657|    func toggleSplitActiveTab() {
475|77cde5|        guard let tabId = activeTabId else { return }
476|4956f0|        guard let idx = tabs.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == tabId }) else { return }
477|adc83b|
478|ae622d|        if tabs[idx].panes.count <= 1 {
479|3f3758|            // Split: add a second pane (max 2 panes for now)
480|47c4fb|            let newPane = TerminalManager()
481|923da3|            newPane.title = "Terminal \(tabs.count).2"
482|692bfb|            tabs[idx].panes.append(newPane)
483|e67696|            tabs[idx].activePaneId = newPane.id
484|b31999|        } else {
485|1a3c65|            // Unsplit: remove all panes except the first
486|6dddf5|            let extraPanes = tabs[idx].panes.dropFirst()
487|669ba4|            for pane in extraPanes {
488|31982c|                pane.disconnect()
489|a7dc16|            }
490|941223|            tabs[idx].panes = Array(tabs[idx].panes.prefix(1))
491|cad079|            tabs[idx].activePaneId = tabs[idx].panes.first?.id ?? tabs[idx].activePaneId
492|5f3077|        }
493|27e597|    }
494|adc83b|
495|e5ad11|    func killActive() {
496|77cde5|        guard let tabId = activeTabId else { return }
497|82eb46|        guard let tabIndex = tabs.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == tabId }) else { return }
498|adc83b|
499|3861ec|        let paneId = tabs[tabIndex].activePaneId
500|3771af|        if tabs[tabIndex].panes.count > 1 {
501|ad5b37|            // If split, kill the active pane only.
502|bf8135|            if let paneIndex = tabs[tabIndex].panes.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == paneId }) {
503|5a8bea|                tabs[tabIndex].panes[paneIndex].disconnect()
504|fed5a3|                tabs[tabIndex].panes.remove(at: paneIndex)
505|a7dc16|            }
506|aa4b79|            tabs[tabIndex].activePaneId = tabs[tabIndex].panes.first?.id ?? tabs[tabIndex].activePaneId
507|adc83b|
508|7f8f51|            if tabs[tabIndex].panes.isEmpty {
509|58d66b|                closeTab(id: tabId)
510|a7dc16|            }
511|b31999|        } else {
512|cb6a91|            // If not split, kill the tab.
513|d69312|            closeTab(id: tabId)
514|5f3077|        }
515|27e597|    }

631|349c34|        return commandHistory[historyIndex]
632|27e597|    }

634|776e44|    func nextCommand() -> String? {
635|110e6c|        guard !commandHistory.isEmpty else { return nil }
636|cfcee6|        historyIndex = min(commandHistory.count, historyIndex + 1)
637|bd9a28|        if historyIndex >= commandHistory.count {
638|273b25|            return ""
639|5f3077|        }
640|349c34|        return commandHistory[historyIndex]
641|27e597|    }
642|b4687f|    
643|9a721f|    private func processLocalCommand(_ command: String) {
644|499317|        let parts = command.split(separator: " ", maxSplits: 1)
645|40788b|        guard let cmd = parts.first?.lowercased() else { return }
646|d6ed84|        
647|c5be0d|        switch cmd {
648|84ac7a|        case "help":
649|e25ab4|            appendOutput("""
650|742a6a|            Local Commands:
651|378490|              help              - Show this help
652|25afb7|              clear             - Clear terminal
653|007b75|              echo <text>       - Echo text
654|5edcc4|              date              - Show current date
655|6ea41d|              whoami            - Show current user
656|36311a|              history           - Show command history
657|9f0baf|              ssh               - Show SSH connection info
658|3070d1|            
659|144f70|            Connect via SSH using the network button in toolbar.
660|4a6995|            Real SSH protocol powered by SwiftNIO SSH.
661|33cb96|            """, type: .output)
662|3070d1|            
663|8d75cb|        case "clear":
664|55c3ab|            clear()
665|3070d1|            
666|629cd7|        case "echo":
667|1b5be1|            let text = parts.count > 1 ? String(parts[1]) : ""
668|b00dd0|            appendOutput(text, type: .output)
669|3070d1|            
670|f72b70|        case "date":
671|4c1e8a|            appendOutput(Date().description, type: .output)
672|3070d1|            
673|492542|        case "whoami":
674|c97efc|            appendOutput("ipad-user", type: .output)
675|3070d1|            
676|06f2cd|        case "history":
677|36fd0c|            for (index, cmd) in commandHistory.enumerated() {
678|c3e90e|                appendOutput("  \(index + 1)  \(cmd)", type: .output)
679|a7dc16|            }
680|3070d1|            
681|2f6c43|        case "ssh":
682|e25ab4|            appendOutput("""
683|558576|            SSH Status: \(isConnected ? "Connected" : "Not connected")
684|9f3dfd|            Implementation: SwiftNIO SSH (apple/swift-nio-ssh)
685|14e2c7|            Features: Password auth, Key auth, PTY support, Shell sessions
686|33cb96|            """, type: .output)
687|3070d1|            
688|520b7d|        default:
689|da445e|            appendOutput("\(cmd): command not found (local mode)", type: .error)
690|5f3077|        }
691|27e597|    }
692|b4687f|    
693|99d6fc|    func appendOutput(_ text: String, type: LineType, isANSI: Bool = false) {
694|0706d6|        DispatchQueue.main.async {
695|c63a2a|            // Split multi-line output into separate lines
696|f7effa|            let lines = text.components(separatedBy: .newlines)
697|1a16f7|            for line in lines {
698|301e4e|                if !line.isEmpty || lines.count == 1 {
699|3609d8|                    self.output.append(TerminalLine(text: line, type: type, isANSI: isANSI || line.contains("\u{1B}")))
700|4e2d32|                }
701|a7dc16|            }
702|5f3077|        }
703|27e597|    }

887|06d184|    private func connect() {
888|5a9168|        errorMessage = nil
889|d6ed84|        
890|d8217a|        let authMethod: SSHConnectionConfig.SSHAuthMethod
891|516cf1|        if useKey {
892|1daa0f|            guard !privateKey.isEmpty else {
893|c56e11|                errorMessage = "Please enter your private key"
894|53ab34|                return
895|a7dc16|            }
896|3aabb2|            authMethod = .privateKey(key: privateKey, passphrase: keyPassphrase.isEmpty ? nil : keyPassphrase)
897|b31999|        } else {
898|0346de|            guard !password.isEmpty else {
899|288d37|                errorMessage = "Please enter your password"
900|53ab34|                return
901|a7dc16|            }
902|99f80b|            authMethod = .password(password)
903|5f3077|        }

906|d6ed84|

908|b71427|            name: name,
909|77bedd|            host: host,
910|39ad81|            port: Int(port) ?? 22,
911|21cc1a|            username: username,
912|f03d4f|            authMethod: authMethod
913|3143a4|        )
914|d6ed84|

916|ce31c3|            connectionStore.save(config)
917|5f3077|        }
918|d6ed84|

920|3a71db|        isPresented = false
921|27e597|    }

949|619a86|struct ANSIText: View {
950|e25e12|    let text: String
951|6f45dc|    @ObservedObject private var themeManager = ThemeManager.shared
952|b4687f|

955|27e597|    }

961|3d9c12|            .textSelection(.enabled)

964|91a22d|    private func stripANSI(_ text: String) -> String {
965|e3c761|        let pattern = "\u{1B}\\[[0-9;]*[a-zA-Z]"
966|d23a93|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern) else { return text }
967|10d615|        let range = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
968|de5100|        return regex.stringByReplacingMatches(in: text, range: range, withTemplate: "")
969|27e597|    }

82|af0ecd|// MARK: - Fuzzy Search
83|adc83b|
84|9fce4f|struct FuzzyMatcher {
85|ae76bd|    static func score(query: String, target: String) -> Int? {
86|34cef6|        guard !query.isEmpty else { return 1000 }
87|d6ed84|        
88|aa4292|        let queryLower = query.lowercased()
89|18ea38|        let targetLower = target.lowercased()
90|d6ed84|        
91|c33784|        // Exact match gets highest score
92|bea5c7|        if targetLower == queryLower { return 10000 }
93|d6ed84|        
94|bffced|        // Contains full query
95|8cd767|        if targetLower.contains(queryLower) {
96|1063f5|            // Bonus for starting with query
97|d0876a|            if targetLower.hasPrefix(queryLower) {
98|2e989d|                return 5000 + (1000 - target.count)
99|a7dc16|            }
100|c9ab09|            return 3000 + (1000 - target.count)
101|5f3077|        }
102|d6ed84|        
103|83786c|        // Fuzzy character matching
104|65f313|        var queryIndex = queryLower.startIndex
105|7f11d4|        var targetIndex = targetLower.startIndex
106|268b95|        var score = 0
107|5dc28e|        var consecutiveBonus = 0
108|1d718f|        var lastMatchIndex: String.Index? = nil
109|d6ed84|        
110|308cfe|        while queryIndex < queryLower.endIndex && targetIndex < targetLower.endIndex {
111|c13bec|            if queryLower[queryIndex] == targetLower[targetIndex] {
112|145bbf|                score += 100 + consecutiveBonus
113|216278|                
114|d6ef12|                // Bonus for consecutive matches
115|9f661a|                if let lastIdx = lastMatchIndex,
116|83874f|                   targetLower.index(after: lastIdx) == targetIndex {
117|9c7108|                    consecutiveBonus += 50
118|fdd0e2|                } else {
119|51d442|                    consecutiveBonus = 0
120|4e2d32|                }
121|216278|                
122|c7d2d9|                // Bonus for matching at word boundaries
123|3c44b0|                if targetIndex == targetLower.startIndex ||
124|75c499|                   !targetLower[targetLower.index(before: targetIndex)].isLetter {
125|78d351|                    score += 75
126|4e2d32|                }
127|216278|                
128|b7133b|                lastMatchIndex = targetIndex
129|ea161d|                queryIndex = queryLower.index(after: queryIndex)
130|a7dc16|            }
131|916731|            targetIndex = targetLower.index(after: targetIndex)
132|5f3077|        }
133|d6ed84|        
134|989e1f|        // All query characters must be found
135|0160b5|        guard queryIndex == queryLower.endIndex else { return nil }
136|d6ed84|        
137|c07521|        return score
138|27e597|    }
139|b4687f|    
140|ace7c9|    static func highlight(query: String, in text: String) -> [(String, Bool)] {
141|81813c|        guard !query.isEmpty else { return [(text, false)] }
142|d6ed84|        
143|b880d0|        var result: [(String, Bool)] = []
144|aa4292|        let queryLower = query.lowercased()
145|a14f23|        let textLower = text.lowercased()
146|d6ed84|        
147|65f313|        var queryIndex = queryLower.startIndex
148|a07ffc|        var currentSegment = ""
149|d3c359|        var isMatch = false
150|d6ed84|        
151|4083e9|        for (i, char) in text.enumerated() {
152|212094|            let textIndex = textLower.index(textLower.startIndex, offsetBy: i)
153|3070d1|            
154|3f747d|            if queryIndex < queryLower.endIndex && 
155|f8248a|               textLower[textIndex] == queryLower[queryIndex] {
156|eecabe|                if !isMatch && !currentSegment.isEmpty {
157|78ec19|                    result.append((currentSegment, false))
158|cc1904|                    currentSegment = ""
159|4e2d32|                }
160|a00101|                isMatch = true
161|b31654|                currentSegment.append(char)
162|ea161d|                queryIndex = queryLower.index(after: queryIndex)
163|f5a6eb|            } else {
164|fbac5d|                if isMatch && !currentSegment.isEmpty {
165|15ba04|                    result.append((currentSegment, true))
166|cc1904|                    currentSegment = ""
167|4e2d32|                }
168|d1cc2f|                isMatch = false
169|b31654|                currentSegment.append(char)
170|a7dc16|            }
171|5f3077|        }
172|d6ed84|        
173|5d8d48|        if !currentSegment.isEmpty {
174|eb146d|            result.append((currentSegment, isMatch))
175|5f3077|        }
176|d6ed84|        
177|67ed82|        return result
178|27e597|    }

40|1b6ea6|// MARK: - Diff Builder (working copy vs HEAD)
41|adc83b|
42|1476f2|private enum _DiffEdit {
43|70b9c9|    case equal(String)
44|d5a877|    case insert(String)
45|4ce584|    case delete(String)
46|b31277|}
47|adc83b|
48|af9510|struct DiffBuilder {
49|0138df|    static func build(fileName: String, status: String, old: String, new: String) -> DiffFile {
50|9e82fa|        let oldLines = splitLines(old)
51|9a046b|        let newLines = splitLines(new)
52|a6deec|        let edits = diffEdits(oldLines, newLines)
53|adc83b|
54|c85a82|        var lines: [DiffLine] = []
55|612c87|        lines.reserveCapacity(edits.count)
56|adc83b|
57|b50bf9|        var oldLineNumber = 1
58|37aaae|        var newLineNumber = 1
59|adc83b|
60|2fed6c|        for edit in edits {
61|8274e4|            switch edit {
62|cc6091|            case let .equal(text):
63|7c5c47|                lines.append(.init(type: .context, content: text, oldLineNumber: oldLineNumber, newLineNumber: newLineNumber))
64|34dd37|                oldLineNumber += 1
65|d0995e|                newLineNumber += 1
66|adc83b|
67|0de55e|            case let .delete(text):
68|a9bb46|                lines.append(.init(type: .deletion, content: text, oldLineNumber: oldLineNumber, newLineNumber: nil))
69|34dd37|                oldLineNumber += 1
70|adc83b|
71|bd8701|            case let .insert(text):
72|cbbb20|                lines.append(.init(type: .addition, content: text, oldLineNumber: nil, newLineNumber: newLineNumber))
73|d0995e|                newLineNumber += 1
74|a7dc16|            }
75|5f3077|        }
76|adc83b|
77|fe8215|        let header = "@@ -1,\(oldLines.count) +1,\(newLines.count) @@"
78|35ffb5|        let hunk = DiffHunk(header: header, lines: lines)
79|6f56c0|        return DiffFile(fileName: fileName, status: status, hunks: [hunk])
80|27e597|    }
81|adc83b|
82|72adbf|    private static func splitLines(_ text: String) -> [String] {
83|9ab348|        var lines = text.components(separatedBy: "\n")
84|b3b18c|        // Drop trailing empty line if file ends with newline.
85|12deaf|        if lines.last == "" {
86|73b25f|            lines.removeLast()
87|5f3077|        }
88|6a8c8e|        return lines
89|27e597|    }
90|adc83b|
91|d861dc|    private static func diffEdits(_ old: [String], _ new: [String]) -> [_DiffEdit] {
92|2ef737|        let n = old.count
93|962d3a|        let m = new.count
94|adc83b|
95|19e396|        if n == 0 { return new.map { .insert($0) } }
96|659f38|        if m == 0 { return old.map { .delete($0) } }
97|adc83b|
98|6d0c13|        // LCS DP (simple + deterministic). Replace with Myers later if needed.
99|249089|        var dp = Array(repeating: Array(repeating: 0, count: m + 1), count: n + 1)
100|da873b|        for i in 1...n {
101|e1eb8d|            for j in 1...m {
102|daa469|                if old[i - 1] == new[j - 1] {
103|59b54f|                    dp[i][j] = dp[i - 1][j - 1] + 1
104|fdd0e2|                } else {
105|ada1d6|                    dp[i][j] = max(dp[i - 1][j], dp[i][j - 1])
106|4e2d32|                }
107|a7dc16|            }
108|5f3077|        }
109|adc83b|
110|c7d097|        var edits: [_DiffEdit] = []
111|30fde6|        edits.reserveCapacity(n + m)
112|adc83b|
113|8f426a|        var i = n
114|2e5d36|        var j = m
115|f21817|        while i > 0 || j > 0 {
116|ff88b1|            if i > 0, j > 0, old[i - 1] == new[j - 1] {
117|3a4cb2|                edits.append(.equal(old[i - 1]))
118|0a3170|                i -= 1
119|038038|                j -= 1
120|314055|            } else if j > 0, i == 0 || dp[i][j - 1] >= dp[i - 1][j] {
121|d7bd75|                edits.append(.insert(new[j - 1]))
122|038038|                j -= 1
123|cbb05a|            } else if i > 0 {
124|218975|                edits.append(.delete(old[i - 1]))
125|0a3170|                i -= 1
126|a7dc16|            }
127|5f3077|        }
128|adc83b|
129|f49266|        return edits.reversed()
130|27e597|    }
131|b31277|}

124|e053f1|    private func diffIndicatorsLayer(minimapHeight: CGFloat, lineCount: Int) -> some View {
125|df88d3|        // VS Code minimap diff markers are thin and pinned to the left.
126|352402|        let barWidth: CGFloat = 2
127|adc83b|
128|eb7497|        // Guard against division by zero
129|dad1b1|        if lineCount > 0 {
130|82ebe9|            ForEach(diffIndicators) { indicator in
131|c4c9a2|                let startLine = max(0, min(indicator.lineRange.lowerBound, lineCount - 1))
132|d34bb2|                let endLineExclusive = max(startLine + 1, min(indicator.lineRange.upperBound, lineCount))
133|adc83b|
134|7e47a5|                let startY = (CGFloat(startLine) / CGFloat(max(lineCount, 1))) * minimapHeight
135|634593|                let endY = (CGFloat(endLineExclusive) / CGFloat(max(lineCount, 1))) * minimapHeight
136|13ec78|                let height = max(2, endY - startY)
137|adc83b|
138|ff13e9|                Rectangle()
139|41dcad|                    .fill(diffColor(for: indicator.kind).opacity(0.95))
140|81c659|                    .frame(width: barWidth, height: height)
141|72358e|                    .offset(x: 0, y: startY)
142|a7dc16|            }
143|5f3077|        }
144|27e597|    }

146|906d12|    // MARK: - Visible region math
147|adc83b|
148|6919f3|    private func visibleRegionHeight(minimapHeight: CGFloat) -> CGFloat {
149|ff17e8|        guard totalContentHeight > 0 else { return 0 }
150|c5f520|        let ratio = scrollViewHeight / totalContentHeight
151|f9bc55|        return minimapHeight * min(max(ratio, 0), 1.0)
152|27e597|    }
153|adc83b|
154|ee5041|    private func visibleRegionOffset(minimapHeight: CGFloat, visibleHeight: CGFloat) -> CGFloat {
155|7da55c|        let scrollable = max(0, totalContentHeight - scrollViewHeight)
156|45fee0|        guard scrollable > 0 else { return 0 }
157|adc83b|
158|e13930|        let scrollRatio = min(max(scrollOffset / scrollable, 0), 1.0)
159|7c51ab|        return scrollRatio * max(0, minimapHeight - visibleHeight)
160|27e597|    }
161|adc83b|
162|04759d|    // MARK: - Interaction
163|adc83b|
164|7ef7ff|    /// Requests scroll so that the main editor's visible region is centered around the minimap Y position.
165|783b1d|    /// Uses callback to parent - minimap never directly controls editor scroll (prevents jitter).
166|92b230|    private func updateScroll(forMinimapY yPosition: CGFloat, minimapHeight: CGFloat) {
167|78fab1|        guard totalContentHeight > 0 else { return }
168|dac0ba|        guard let onScrollRequested = onScrollRequested else { return }
169|adc83b|
170|783533|        let clampedY = max(0, min(yPosition, minimapHeight))
171|89fa92|        let ratio = (minimapHeight > 0) ? (clampedY / minimapHeight) : 0
172|adc83b|
173|e4e280|        // Target a center position (VS Code behavior).
174|3b7590|        let targetCenter = ratio * totalContentHeight
175|b9ce99|        let desiredOffset = targetCenter - (scrollViewHeight / 2)
176|adc83b|
177|5b5c2d|        let maxOffset = max(0, totalContentHeight - scrollViewHeight)
178|6a7c82|        let newOffset = min(max(desiredOffset, 0), maxOffset)
179|d6ed84|        
180|73b1e7|        // Request scroll via callback - parent controls the actual scroll
181|f186d0|        onScrollRequested(newOffset)
182|27e597|    }
183|adc83b|
184|57db31|    // MARK: - Rendering (Canvas)
185|adc83b|
186|ddfd07|    private func drawMinimapPreview(
187|1dbb0f|        in context: inout GraphicsContext,
188|8ae978|        size: CGSize,
189|e54bca|        lines: [Substring]
190|981e04|    ) {
191|c96a6f|        let paddingX: CGFloat = 4
192|435081|        let paddingY: CGFloat = 2
193|adc83b|
194|c711e9|        let contentWidth = max(0, size.width - (paddingX * 2))
195|6c41d9|        let contentHeight = max(0, size.height - (paddingY * 2))
196|adc83b|
197|82f19e|        guard contentWidth > 0, contentHeight > 0 else { return }
198|adc83b|
199|ad5ba7|        let lineCount = max(lines.count, 1)
200|d6ed84|        
201|02e15c|        // FIXED: Use fixed pixels per line (VS Code style) instead of stretching to fill
202|54f182|        // This ensures the minimap always shows a tiny preview regardless of file size
203|3065bb|        let targetPixelsPerLine: CGFloat = 2.5
204|7dd91a|        let pixelsPerLine = targetPixelsPerLine
205|d6ed84|        
206|9b2a64|        // Calculate how many lines we can show in the minimap
207|3e694e|        let visibleLines = Int(contentHeight / pixelsPerLine)
208|d6ed84|        
209|1d6fd4|        // Calculate scroll offset to show the right portion of the document
210|91f804|        // Use scrollOffset and totalContentHeight to calculate current position
211|738fb2|        let scrollRatio = totalContentHeight > 0 ? Double(scrollOffset) / Double(max(totalContentHeight - scrollViewHeight, 1)) : 0
212|5d3dc8|        let startLine = max(0, Int(scrollRatio * Double(max(0, lineCount - visibleLines))))
213|adc83b|
214|03dc30|        // Token-block mode (colored rectangles) - VS Code style minimap
215|200364|        let minBarHeight: CGFloat = 1
216|f6b381|        let barHeight = max(minBarHeight, pixelsPerLine)
217|adc83b|
218|d1e35f|        // Approximate "characters" across minimap width.
219|26fc02|        let maxChars: CGFloat = 120
220|64e37a|        let charWidth = contentWidth / maxChars
221|adc83b|
222|dd472a|        // Render lines starting from startLine (scrolls with document)
223|8082c0|        let endLine = min(startLine + visibleLines + 1, lineCount)
224|d6ed84|        
225|5be8fa|        // Guard against invalid range (endLine must be >= startLine)
226|4957c8|        guard endLine >= startLine else { return }
227|d6ed84|        
228|714e33|        for i in startLine..<endLine {
229|794e26|            let displayIndex = i - startLine
230|82adeb|            let y = paddingY + (CGFloat(displayIndex) * pixelsPerLine)
231|db9e6f|            if y > size.height { break }
232|adc83b|
233|87a58d|            let line = lines.indices.contains(i) ? lines[i] : Substring("")
234|1922e4|            let tokens = tokenize(line)
235|adc83b|
236|ed9464|            var x = paddingX
237|4f7785|            let yAligned = y.rounded(FloatingPointRoundingRule.down)
238|adc83b|
239|993665|            if tokens.isEmpty {
240|e53354|                // Render faint whitespace line.
241|852310|                let rect = CGRect(x: x, y: yAligned, width: max(4, contentWidth * 0.15), height: barHeight)
242|afc890|                context.fill(Path(rect), with: .color(Color(white: 0.45).opacity(0.10)))
243|1df510|                continue
244|a7dc16|            }
245|adc83b|
246|3f8f53|            for token in tokens {
247|0ef518|                guard x < (paddingX + contentWidth) else { break }
248|6f9f42|                let w = max(1, CGFloat(token.text.count) * charWidth)
249|4a0a54|                let rect = CGRect(x: x, y: yAligned, width: min(w, paddingX + contentWidth - x), height: barHeight)
250|0a74f9|                context.fill(Path(rect), with: .color(token.color.opacity(0.80)))
251|354777|                x += w
252|a7dc16|            }
253|5f3077|        }
254|27e597|    }

301|e5b85c|            // Preserve a tiny amount of "whitespace presence" so empty lines still show.
302|9dd08f|            var chunk = AttributedString(" ")
303|9befb1|            chunk.font = .system(size: fontSize, weight: .regular, design: .monospaced)
304|8cb2a3|            chunk.foregroundColor = Color(white: 0.7).opacity(0.25)

307|adc83b|

309|27e597|    }
310|adc83b|
311|4abcd7|    private func tokenize(_ line: Substring) -> [Token] {
312|f0a25f|        // Extremely lightweight tokenizer:
313|6188fb|        // - full-line comment if first non-space is # (python-like)
314|de2ec8|        // - inline comment starting at //
315|0a0697|        // - strings in "..." or '...'
316|efb1f5|        // - numbers
317|23cdc0|        // - keywords
318|43ec2e|        // - PascalCase tokens treated as type names
319|39dd2a|        var tokens: [Token] = []
320|3d99ce|        var i = line.startIndex
321|adc83b|
322|600872|        func peek(_ offset: Int = 0) -> Character? {
323|34ecda|            var idx = i
324|c6ee90|            for _ in 0..<offset {
325|2838dc|                guard idx < line.endIndex else { return nil }
326|306cea|                idx = line.index(after: idx)
327|a7dc16|            }
328|5bdcc9|            return idx < line.endIndex ? line[idx] : nil
329|5f3077|        }
330|adc83b|
331|5ea689|        func advance(_ n: Int = 1) {
332|293115|            for _ in 0..<n {
333|42c484|                guard i < line.endIndex else { return }
334|10bf0b|                i = line.index(after: i)
335|a7dc16|            }
336|5f3077|        }
337|adc83b|
338|80ae1a|        // Detect python/shebang-like comment lines: first non-whitespace is '#'
339|5015b2|        if let firstNonSpace = line.firstIndex(where: { !$0.isWhitespace }),
340|fc3e36|           line[firstNonSpace] == "#" {
341|a7cd18|            tokens.append(Token(text: line[line.startIndex..<line.endIndex], kind: .comment))
342|41c689|            return tokens
343|5f3077|        }
344|adc83b|
345|544fab|        while i < line.endIndex {
346|7e4e40|            let ch = line[i]
347|adc83b|
348|40eeea|            // Inline comment: //
349|8fbe15|            if ch == "/", peek(1) == "/" {
350|860932|                let range = i..<line.endIndex
351|b67a6a|                tokens.append(Token(text: line[range], kind: .comment))
352|23d68f|                return tokens
353|a7dc16|            }
354|adc83b|
355|41a694|            // Whitespace
356|76957e|            if ch.isWhitespace {
357|eae3bb|                let start = i
358|7f4f8a|                while i < line.endIndex, line[i].isWhitespace { advance() }
359|3f1e7d|                tokens.append(Token(text: line[start..<i], kind: .plain))
360|1df510|                continue
361|a7dc16|            }
362|adc83b|
363|e53ff2|            // String literals
364|899c9c|            if ch == "\"" || ch == "'" {
365|9d8090|                let quote = ch
366|eae3bb|                let start = i
367|e2aa2f|                advance()
368|4ed8ff|                var escaped = false
369|3876db|                while i < line.endIndex {
370|9c755e|                    let c = line[i]
371|605f4e|                    if escaped {
372|cb9c8a|                        escaped = false
373|3f9321|                        advance()
374|e47242|                        continue
375|c9717a|                    }
376|7f8424|                    if c == "\\" {
377|37863a|                        escaped = true
378|3f9321|                        advance()
379|e47242|                        continue
380|c9717a|                    }
381|d1886f|                    if c == quote {
382|3f9321|                        advance()
383|28a64b|                        break
384|c9717a|                    }
385|7c96dd|                    advance()
386|4e2d32|                }
387|9305c9|                tokens.append(Token(text: line[start..<i], kind: .string))
388|1df510|                continue
389|a7dc16|            }
390|adc83b|
391|bd52f1|            // Numbers
392|38cd36|            if ch.isNumber {
393|eae3bb|                let start = i
394|89de1b|                while i < line.endIndex, line[i].isNumber || line[i] == "." { advance() }
395|8480cb|                tokens.append(Token(text: line[start..<i], kind: .number))
396|1df510|                continue
397|a7dc16|            }
398|adc83b|
399|1b4cce|            // Identifiers / keywords
400|181e74|            if ch.isLetter || ch == "_" {
401|eae3bb|                let start = i
402|e2aa2f|                advance()
403|3876db|                while i < line.endIndex {
404|9c755e|                    let c = line[i]
405|e225c5|                    if c.isLetter || c.isNumber || c == "_" { advance() } else { break }
406|4e2d32|                }
407|cd95c9|                let word = line[start..<i]
408|8aa092|                let kind: Token.Kind
409|adc83b|
410|08878f|                if isKeyword(word) {
411|74c41d|                    kind = .keyword
412|be7b6b|                } else if looksLikeTypeName(word) {
413|00ef8c|                    kind = .typeName
414|fdd0e2|                } else {
415|d46347|                    kind = .plain
416|4e2d32|                }
417|adc83b|
418|d43ef3|                tokens.append(Token(text: word, kind: kind))
419|1df510|                continue
420|a7dc16|            }
421|adc83b|
422|612c55|            // Operators / punctuation
423|953483|            let start = i
424|acf00b|            advance()
425|f768b8|            tokens.append(Token(text: line[start..<i], kind: .plain))
426|5f3077|        }
427|adc83b|
428|50a443|        return tokens
429|27e597|    }
430|adc83b|
431|3facb7|    private func isKeyword(_ word: Substring) -> Bool {
432|c4f25e|        // Small superset of common Swift/JS/Python keywords.
433|b2b9d9|        // (We can't depend on a full parser here.)
434|396c95|        let keywords: Set<String> = [
435|9af6d0|            "import", "export", "from", "as",
436|dbd304|            "struct", "class", "enum", "protocol", "extension", "func", "var", "let",
437|bd4ed1|            "if", "else", "for", "while", "repeat", "switch", "case", "default",
438|e351bd|            "break", "continue", "return", "throw", "throws", "try", "catch",
439|b9f132|            "do", "in", "where", "guard", "defer",
440|511559|            "public", "private", "fileprivate", "internal", "open",
441|12dd92|            "static", "final", "override", "mutating", "nonmutating",
442|91d838|            "async", "await",
443|6f6f8c|            "true", "false", "nil",
444|0cf8cf|            "self", "super",
445|e39cc4|            // JS/Python-ish
446|ad9513|            "const", "function", "async", "await", "new", "this",
447|1c9b9e|            "def", "pass", "lambda", "None"
448|220505|        ]
449|0da584|        return keywords.contains(String(word))
450|27e597|    }
451|adc83b|
452|e0492d|    private func looksLikeTypeName(_ word: Substring) -> Bool {
453|ce64a9|        // Simple heuristic: PascalCase (leading uppercase).
454|bbf2da|        guard let first = word.first else { return false }
455|248546|        return first.isUppercase
456|27e597|    }

187|3b223e|    private var diffGutter: some View {
188|8eb6a2|        GeometryReader { _ in
189|f47dba|            Canvas { context, size in
190|f2e3c7|                guard !visibleLineRange.isEmpty else { return }
191|adc83b|
192|1d1279|                let w = size.width
193|6cfee9|                let corner = configuration.gutterCornerRadius
194|adc83b|
195|c4be89|                for line in visibleLineRange {
196|1a6571|                    if let kind = changesByLine[line] {
197|7acfe4|                        let y = contentTopInset + CGFloat(line - visibleLineRange.lowerBound) * lineHeight
198|398690|                        let rect = CGRect(x: 0, y: y, width: w, height: max(1, lineHeight))
199|3e9bba|                        let path = Path(roundedRect: rect, cornerRadius: corner)
200|d14140|                        context.fill(path, with: .color(color(for: kind)))
201|c9717a|                    }
202|adc83b|
203|d80c45|                    // Deleted markers are drawn as triangles at the boundary.
204|d77c52|                    if deletedMarkers.contains(line) {
205|7acfe4|                        let y = contentTopInset + CGFloat(line - visibleLineRange.lowerBound) * lineHeight
206|f6ef50|                        var p = Path()
207|9c8d93|                        p.move(to: CGPoint(x: 0, y: y))
208|6c103f|                        p.addLine(to: CGPoint(x: w, y: y + (lineHeight * 0.5)))
209|4b3b60|                        p.addLine(to: CGPoint(x: 0, y: y + lineHeight))
210|eef458|                        p.closeSubpath()
211|c248e0|                        context.fill(p, with: .color(configuration.deletedColor))
212|c9717a|                    }
213|4e2d32|                }
214|a7dc16|            }

261|1950d9|    // MARK: Reload
262|adc83b|
263|0fd45c|    @MainActor
264|fb91cc|    private func reloadAll(force: Bool) async {
265|6deaac|        // Diff
266|40a056|        if configuration.showsDiffIndicators {
267|71cc09|            do {
268|fca72e|                let diff = try await dataSource.diff(fileURL, force)
269|6e72ba|                var byLine: [Int: GitLineChangeKind] = [:]
270|9310cd|                var deletions: Set<Int> = []
271|adc83b|
272|fa601b|                for c in diff {
273|c2ffec|                    switch c.kind {
274|824c69|                    case .deleted:
275|590b9b|                        deletions.insert(max(1, c.line))
276|7f90ef|                    case .added, .modified:

293|ba24de|                self.blameByLine = Dictionary(uniqueKeysWithValues: blame.map { ($0.line, $0) })
294|91b9a2|            } catch {

317|e83eda|private struct GitShell {
318|36bf91|    static func runGit(args: [String], in workingDirectory: URL) async throws -> String {
319|fb15d6|        #if os(macOS) || targetEnvironment(macCatalyst) || os(Linux)
320|c9b222|        return try await withCheckedThrowingContinuation { cont in
321|13023b|            let process = Process()
322|9dce62|            process.executableURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: "/usr/bin/env")
323|6980d1|            process.arguments = ["git"] + args
324|349037|            process.currentDirectoryURL = workingDirectory
325|adc83b|
326|440eab|            let outPipe = Pipe()
327|7e6031|            let errPipe = Pipe()
328|a6bd70|            process.standardOutput = outPipe
329|203afe|            process.standardError = errPipe
330|adc83b|
331|71cc09|            do {
332|eee8fb|                try process.run()
333|91b9a2|            } catch {
334|1d8745|                cont.resume(throwing: GitError.commandFailed("Unable to launch git"))
335|53ab34|                return
336|a7dc16|            }
337|adc83b|
338|2d3dad|            process.terminationHandler = { p in
339|ac2e77|                let outData = outPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
340|b22e9b|                let errData = errPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
341|adc83b|
342|b7139c|                let out = String(data: outData, encoding: .utf8) ?? ""
343|3079dc|                let err = String(data: errData, encoding: .utf8) ?? ""
344|adc83b|
345|4e1e82|                if p.terminationStatus == 0 {
346|a411dd|                    cont.resume(returning: out)
347|fdd0e2|                } else {
348|1759a5|                    let msg = err.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
349|4befeb|                    cont.resume(throwing: GitError.commandFailed(msg.isEmpty ? out : msg))
350|4e2d32|                }
351|a7dc16|            }
352|5f3077|        }
353|f6012e|        #else
354|459a57|        throw GitError.commandFailed("Git execution is not available on this platform")
355|6a3e13|        #endif
356|27e597|    }
357|adc83b|
358|ce4ef6|    static func repoRoot(containing fileURL: URL) async throws -> URL {
359|912523|        let dir = fileURL.deletingLastPathComponent()
360|1a9799|        let out = try await runGit(args: ["-C", dir.path, "rev-parse", "--show-toplevel"], in: dir)
361|fe3a8f|        let rootPath = out.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
362|58de76|        if rootPath.isEmpty { throw GitError.notARepository }
363|564829|        return URL(fileURLWithPath: rootPath)
364|27e597|    }

371|adc83b|

373|adc83b|
374|348ef2|    func invalidate(forFile fileURL: URL) async {
375|4da690|        do {

377|c274c2|            let relPath = Self.relativePath(fileURL, repoRoot)
378|37ccff|            let key = repoRoot.path + "::" + relPath
379|5c07e2|            cache.removeValue(forKey: key)
380|853889|        } catch {
381|0ef52b|            // ignore
382|5f3077|        }
383|27e597|    }
384|adc83b|
385|5ad013|    func lineChanges(forFile fileURL: URL) async throws -> [GitLineChange] {
386|84184f|        let repoRoot = try await GitShell.repoRoot(containing: fileURL)
387|7cb904|        let relPath = Self.relativePath(fileURL, repoRoot)
388|471cce|        let key = repoRoot.path + "::" + relPath
389|adc83b|
390|04a632|        if let cached = cache[key] { return cached }
391|adc83b|
392|18475b|        // Unified=0 makes hunks contain only the changed lines, simplifying mapping.
393|471a19|        let diff = try await GitShell.runGit(
394|0211d7|            args: ["-C", repoRoot.path, "diff", "--unified=0", "--no-color", "--", relPath],
395|2f85ba|            in: repoRoot
396|3143a4|        )
397|adc83b|
398|cb6bb6|        let parsed = Self.parseUnifiedZeroDiff(diff)
399|fd7b4b|        cache[key] = parsed
400|4686f7|        return parsed
401|27e597|    }
402|adc83b|
403|7f38bd|    fileprivate static func relativePath(_ fileURL: URL, _ repoRoot: URL) -> String {
404|d34cf8|        let filePath = fileURL.standardizedFileURL.path
405|d236cb|        let rootPath = repoRoot.standardizedFileURL.path
406|87d341|        if filePath.hasPrefix(rootPath + "/") {
407|c8ae11|            return String(filePath.dropFirst(rootPath.count + 1))
408|5f3077|        }
409|231fb2|        return fileURL.lastPathComponent
410|27e597|    }
411|adc83b|
412|4ab2d0|    /// Parse output from: `git diff --unified=0 --no-color -- <file>`.
413|2cbc84|    ///
414|043652|    /// Heuristic classification per hunk:
415|e6cab5|    /// - oldCount==0,newCount>0 -> .added on new range
416|830185|    /// - oldCount>0,newCount>0 -> .modified on new range
417|d827b0|    /// - oldCount>0,newCount==0 -> .deleted marker at newStart
418|e30ee3|    private static func parseUnifiedZeroDiff(_ text: String) -> [GitLineChange] {
419|0c442a|        var results: [GitLineChange] = []
420|adc83b|
421|5283b2|        // Example hunk header (unified=0):
422|61ad0c|        // @@ -12,2 +12,3 @@
423|960d91|        // or @@ -12 +12 @@
424|53c1fb|        for raw in text.split(separator: "\n", omittingEmptySubsequences: false) {
425|338332|            let line = String(raw)
426|566e9f|            guard line.hasPrefix("@@"), let h = parseHunkHeader(line) else { continue }
427|adc83b|
428|ce5131|            if h.oldCount == 0 && h.newCount > 0 {
429|5447be|                for n in 0..<h.newCount {
430|c93a02|                    results.append(.init(line: h.newStart + n, kind: .added))
431|4e2d32|                }
432|688fe3|            } else if h.oldCount > 0 && h.newCount > 0 {
433|5447be|                for n in 0..<h.newCount {
434|9de390|                    results.append(.init(line: h.newStart + n, kind: .modified))
435|4e2d32|                }
436|b8c2f6|            } else if h.oldCount > 0 && h.newCount == 0 {
437|d2860f|                results.append(.init(line: max(1, h.newStart), kind: .deleted))
438|a7dc16|            }
439|5f3077|        }
440|adc83b|
441|877b21|        // De-dupe (prefer modified over added if collision).
442|d9be21|        var byLine: [Int: GitLineChangeKind] = [:]
443|9c02f9|        var deleted: Set<Int> = []
444|6ab11d|        for r in results {
445|b275dd|            switch r.kind {
446|e08d5d|            case .deleted:
447|22dea6|                deleted.insert(r.line)
448|0ad1c2|            case .added:
449|2faf5e|                if byLine[r.line] == nil { byLine[r.line] = .added }
450|909e67|            case .modified:
451|35bde7|                byLine[r.line] = .modified
452|a7dc16|            }
453|5f3077|        }
454|adc83b|
455|cbba29|        var merged: [GitLineChange] = []
456|8455c8|        for (line, kind) in byLine { merged.append(.init(line: line, kind: kind)) }
457|303285|        for d in deleted { merged.append(.init(line: d, kind: .deleted)) }
458|adc83b|
459|2c2d8a|        return merged.sorted { $0.line < $1.line }
460|27e597|    }
461|adc83b|
462|04b6a6|    private struct Hunk {
463|703f57|        var oldStart: Int
464|9021d9|        var oldCount: Int
465|5918d9|        var newStart: Int
466|c74eb3|        var newCount: Int
467|27e597|    }
468|adc83b|
469|c5499e|    private static func parseHunkHeader(_ header: String) -> Hunk? {
470|ba73ec|        // Header format: @@ -oldStart,oldCount +newStart,newCount @@ ...
471|7417bc|        // Counts may be omitted: -12 +12
472|ecf5bf|        guard let rangeStart = header.range(of: "@@") else { return nil }
473|7c0e7f|        guard let rangeEnd = header.range(of: "@@", options: [], range: rangeStart.upperBound..<header.endIndex) else { return nil }
474|8445bb|        let body = header[rangeStart.upperBound..<rangeEnd.lowerBound].trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces)
475|adc83b|
476|d7518c|        let parts = body.split(separator: " ")
477|246d66|        guard parts.count >= 2 else { return nil }
478|adc83b|
479|305ea0|        func parsePart(_ s: Substring, prefix: Character) -> (Int, Int)? {
480|358d18|            guard s.first == prefix else { return nil }
481|f55934|            let rest = s.dropFirst()
482|66d2d2|            if let comma = rest.firstIndex(of: ",") {
483|8b33f9|                let a = rest[..<comma]
484|95dc6a|                let b = rest[rest.index(after: comma)...]
485|17c68e|                guard let start = Int(a), let count = Int(b) else { return nil }
486|08311d|                return (start, count)
487|f5a6eb|            } else {
488|104757|                guard let start = Int(rest) else { return nil }
489|b303d1|                return (start, 1)
490|a7dc16|            }
491|5f3077|        }
492|adc83b|
493|c2352c|        guard let old = parsePart(parts[0], prefix: "-") else { return nil }
494|868552|        guard let new = parsePart(parts[1], prefix: "+") else { return nil }
495|1713af|        return Hunk(oldStart: old.0, oldCount: old.1, newStart: new.0, newCount: new.1)
496|27e597|    }
497|b31277|}
498|adc83b|
499|a7cfe8|// MARK: - Blame

514|5f3077|        }

517|102596|    func blame(forFile fileURL: URL) async throws -> [GitBlameLine] {
518|84184f|        let repoRoot = try await GitShell.repoRoot(containing: fileURL)
519|be393e|        let relPath = GitDiffService.relativePath(fileURL, repoRoot)

523|adc83b|
524|5df987|        let out = try await GitShell.runGit(

526|2f85ba|            in: repoRoot
