533|adc83b|
534|5b8e3d|    private static func parseLinePorcelain(_ text: String) -> [GitBlameLine] {
535|df70a3|        // Format (porcelain):
536|d0babc|        // <sha> <origLine> <finalLine> <numLines>
537|fd523f|        // author <name>
538|407206|        // author-time <unix>
539|6d5fc5|        // summary <text>
540|ee16bf|        // ...
541|312b42|        // \t<source line>
542|47e69c|        // (then additional \t lines if <numLines> > 1)
543|adc83b|
544|ea5373|        var results: [GitBlameLine] = []
545|adc83b|
546|08428a|        var currentCommit: String = ""
547|6a21c1|        var currentAuthor: String = ""
548|edf098|        var currentAuthorTime: Date?
549|a1305c|        var currentSummary: String = ""
550|adc83b|
551|8b0ddd|        var pendingFinalLine: Int?
552|afb9b4|        var pendingRemaining: Int = 0
553|adc83b|
554|79246a|        func isHexString(_ s: Substring) -> Bool {
555|9e5fb7|            !s.isEmpty && s.allSatisfy { $0.isHexDigit }
556|5f3077|        }
557|adc83b|
558|1b00b6|        func emitOneLineIfPossible() {
559|0a458d|            guard pendingRemaining > 0,
560|99e082|                  let ln = pendingFinalLine,
561|56bbe2|                  !currentCommit.isEmpty else { return }
562|adc83b|
563|fd4da5|            results.append(
564|097c0e|                GitBlameLine(
565|6f7c36|                    line: ln,
566|26bf7c|                    commit: currentCommit,
567|3662a1|                    author: currentAuthor,
568|50c5da|                    authorTime: currentAuthorTime,
569|dd93dd|                    summary: currentSummary
570|6f642e|                )
571|43d041|            )
572|adc83b|
573|0b9ee3|            pendingFinalLine = ln + 1
574|c7cebe|            pendingRemaining -= 1
575|adc83b|
576|c83759|            if pendingRemaining == 0 {
577|f88042|                pendingFinalLine = nil
578|eba976|                currentCommit = ""
579|0d42dc|                currentAuthor = ""
580|0715f9|                currentAuthorTime = nil
581|33c8d7|                currentSummary = ""
582|a7dc16|            }
583|5f3077|        }
584|adc83b|
585|53c1fb|        for raw in text.split(separator: "\n", omittingEmptySubsequences: false) {
586|338332|            let line = String(raw)
587|adc83b|
588|251111|            if line.hasPrefix("\t") {
589|001c3e|                emitOneLineIfPossible()
590|1df510|                continue
591|a7dc16|            }
592|adc83b|
593|6aa6c7|            // Header line:
594|44d4c8|            // <sha> <origLine> <finalLine> <numLines>
595|ac0a66|            // (some variants may omit <numLines>; treat as 1)
596|cbc8d9|            let parts = line.split(separator: " ")
597|5ce5e6|            if parts.count >= 3,
598|8abcbe|               isHexString(parts[0]),
599|f49573|               Int(parts[1]) != nil,
600|f170d7|               let final = Int(parts[2]) {
601|f1b98a|                currentCommit = String(parts[0])
602|ab622d|                pendingFinalLine = final
603|189881|                pendingRemaining = (parts.count >= 4 ? Int(parts[3]) : nil) ?? 1
604|1df510|                continue
605|a7dc16|            }
606|adc83b|
607|77e2a1|            if line.hasPrefix("author ") {
608|d4a57a|                currentAuthor = String(line.dropFirst("author ".count))
609|6a62c8|            } else if line.hasPrefix("author-time ") {
610|4416ac|                let ts = String(line.dropFirst("author-time ".count))
611|39954c|                if let t = TimeInterval(ts) {
612|d16dcd|                    currentAuthorTime = Date(timeIntervalSince1970: t)
613|4e2d32|                }
614|f4e3fa|            } else if line.hasPrefix("summary ") {
615|a63d16|                currentSummary = String(line.dropFirst("summary ".count))
616|a7dc16|            }
617|5f3077|        }
618|adc83b|
619|e40d81|        return results.sorted { $0.line < $1.line }
620|27e597|    }

31|504e43|    var body: some View {
32|151fd5|        GeometryReader { geo in
33|fd8d27|            let font = UIFont.monospacedSystemFont(ofSize: fontSize, weight: .regular)
34|36c5e7|            let charWidth = (" " as NSString).size(withAttributes: [.font: font]).width
35|1c711a|            let fontLineHeight = font.lineHeight
36|94577f|            let baselineAdjustment = max(0, (lineHeight - fontLineHeight) / 2)
37|20c353|            let maxVisibleLines = Int(ceil(geo.size.height / max(lineHeight, 1))) + 2
38|adc83b|
39|7ee956|            let lines = code.components(separatedBy: .newlines)
40|adc83b|
41|8fd116|            ZStack(alignment: .topLeading) {
42|bfb2c3|                ForEach(hints) { hint in
43|d11cfb|                    if hint.line >= scrollPosition && hint.line <= (scrollPosition + maxVisibleLines) {

46|adc83b|

71|27e597|    }

77|211bd1|    private func visualColumn(in line: String, utf16Column: Int, tabSize: Int) -> Int {

79|0e6566|        let clamped = max(0, min(utf16Column, ns.length))

89|5f3077|        }

115|4a4aa9|        let sourcePane = fromPaneId.flatMap { id in panes.first { $0.id == id } } ?? activePane
116|d018e4|        guard let source = sourcePane else { return }
117|d6ed84|        
118|ecd130|        // Create new pane with duplicate of active tab (or empty)
119|403ac4|        var newTabs: [Tab] = []
120|e7a36d|        if let activeTab = source.activeTab {
121|561680|            let duplicateTab = Tab(
122|738907|                fileName: activeTab.fileName,

125|664421|                url: activeTab.url,

135|d6ed84|

138|0a032c|        splitRatios = Array(repeating: ratio, count: panes.count)
139|d6ed84|

141|27e597|    }

143|0e5294|    func closePane(id: UUID) {
144|0340ad|        guard panes.count > 1 else { return } // Keep at least one pane
145|653e9e|        guard let index = panes.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == id }) else { return }
146|d6ed84|        
147|6e551e|        panes.remove(at: index)
148|c30876|        splitRatios.remove(at: index)
149|d6ed84|

151|7df9cd|        let total = splitRatios.reduce(0, +)
152|a5f33f|        if total > 0 {
153|e10388|            splitRatios = splitRatios.map { $0 / total }
154|b31999|        } else {

156|5f3077|        }
157|d6ed84|

159|d0cbf9|        if activePaneId == id {

161|5f3077|        }
162|27e597|    }

199|0a032c|        splitRatios = Array(repeating: ratio, count: panes.count)
200|6ae100|        activePaneId = newPane.id
201|27e597|    }
202|b4687f|    
203|fc4e2f|    func updateRatio(at index: Int, delta: CGFloat, totalSize: CGFloat) {
204|aa52a4|        guard index < splitRatios.count - 1 else { return }
205|d6ed84|        
206|f7ce87|        let deltaRatio = delta / totalSize
207|019df3|        let minRatio: CGFloat = 0.15
208|d6ed84|        
209|3f9e36|        let newRatio1 = splitRatios[index] + deltaRatio
210|d4621b|        let newRatio2 = splitRatios[index + 1] - deltaRatio
211|d6ed84|        
212|289da5|        if newRatio1 >= minRatio && newRatio2 >= minRatio {
213|6df122|            splitRatios[index] = newRatio1
214|7b2474|            splitRatios[index + 1] = newRatio2
215|5f3077|        }
216|27e597|    }

101|b4687f|    
102|aeac0d|    private static func parseSwiftSymbols(from content: String) -> [CodeSymbol] {
103|08506f|        var symbols: [CodeSymbol] = []
104|228023|        let lines = content.components(separatedBy: .newlines)
105|d6ed84|        
106|bc1385|        let patterns: [(pattern: String, type: SymbolType)] = [
107|fc8340|            // Functions
108|c10247|            (#"^\s*(public |private |internal |fileprivate |open )?func\s+(\w+)"#, .function),
109|8fed15|            // Classes
110|420729|            (#"^\s*(public |private |internal |fileprivate |open )?(final )?class\s+(\w+)"#, .class),
111|2f60d1|            // Structs
112|f75c05|            (#"^\s*(public |private |internal |fileprivate |open )?struct\s+(\w+)"#, .struct),
113|af4603|            // Enums
114|1468c0|            (#"^\s*(public |private |internal |fileprivate |open )?enum\s+(\w+)"#, .enum),
115|2fc5af|            // Protocols
116|48e586|            (#"^\s*(public |private |internal |fileprivate |open )?protocol\s+(\w+)"#, .protocol),
117|f5d37b|            // Properties
118|dc53a3|            (#"^\s*(public |private |internal |fileprivate |open )?(static |class )?(var|let)\s+(\w+)"#, .property),
119|235e1d|            // Init
120|7630ef|            (#"^\s*(public |private |internal |fileprivate |open )?(required |convenience )?init"#, .constructor),
121|220505|        ]
122|d6ed84|        
123|d1a1ab|        for (lineIndex, line) in lines.enumerated() {
124|3a36dc|            for (pattern, type) in patterns {
125|66048b|                if let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern, options: []),
126|0483e7|                   let match = regex.firstMatch(in: line, options: [], range: NSRange(line.startIndex..., in: line)) {
127|dd2193|                    
128|277cff|                    var name: String
129|dd2193|                    
130|973af5|                    // Extract the name based on type
131|95923a|                    if type == .constructor {
132|932c3b|                        name = "init"
133|6f3cd6|                        // Try to get parameters
134|2dcc0c|                        if let parenRange = line.range(of: "(") {
135|f790c1|                            let afterParen = String(line[parenRange.lowerBound...])
136|5f45d4|                            if let closeRange = afterParen.range(of: ")") {
137|3abd65|                                let params = String(afterParen[afterParen.index(after: afterParen.startIndex)..<closeRange.lowerBound])
138|95cae0|                                if !params.isEmpty {
139|c5f767|                                    name = "init(\(params.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces)))"
140|f83e05|                                }
141|89d40a|                            }
142|392b35|                        }
143|540066|                    } else {
144|da86c9|                        // Get the last capture group which should be the name
145|769896|                        let lastGroupIndex = match.numberOfRanges - 1
146|170684|                        if lastGroupIndex > 0,
147|e5e5c3|                           let range = Range(match.range(at: lastGroupIndex), in: line) {
148|155a4b|                            name = String(line[range])
149|65e2f4|                        } else {
150|84d6cb|                            continue
151|392b35|                        }
152|c9717a|                    }
153|dd2193|                    
154|62536b|                    symbols.append(CodeSymbol(
155|e8eb2a|                        name: name,
156|dd7229|                        type: type,
157|35d8e4|                        line: lineIndex + 1,
158|6aead8|                        column: 1,
159|56d74d|                        detail: nil,
160|4b2c23|                        containerName: nil
161|c89922|                    ))
162|8dcb2c|                    break
163|4e2d32|                }
164|a7dc16|            }
165|5f3077|        }
166|d6ed84|        
167|1e442a|        return symbols
168|27e597|    }

171|b4687f|    
172|ab4b8c|    private static func parseJSSymbols(from content: String) -> [CodeSymbol] {
173|08506f|        var symbols: [CodeSymbol] = []
174|228023|        let lines = content.components(separatedBy: .newlines)
175|d6ed84|        
176|bc1385|        let patterns: [(pattern: String, type: SymbolType)] = [
177|fc8340|            // Functions
178|6686a3|            (#"^\s*(export )?(async )?function\s+(\w+)"#, .function),
179|90b7a5|            // Arrow functions assigned to const/let
180|46538c|            (#"^\s*(export )?(const|let|var)\s+(\w+)\s*=\s*(async )?\(.*\)\s*=>"#, .function),
181|8fed15|            // Classes
182|b5230a|            (#"^\s*(export )?(default )?class\s+(\w+)"#, .class),
183|48ca72|            // Interfaces (TypeScript)
184|8f0c51|            (#"^\s*(export )?interface\s+(\w+)"#, .interface),
185|45f8e1|            // Types (TypeScript)
186|df9f56|            (#"^\s*(export )?type\s+(\w+)"#, .type),
187|3a9a71|            // Enums (TypeScript)
188|5b99c6|            (#"^\s*(export )?enum\s+(\w+)"#, .enum),
189|6dc670|            // Const/Let/Var
190|6edc9a|            (#"^\s*(export )?(const|let|var)\s+(\w+)\s*="#, .variable),
191|5adad0|            // Methods in class
192|dfbfee|            (#"^\s*(static )?(async )?(\w+)\s*\(.*\)\s*\{"#, .method),
193|220505|        ]
194|d6ed84|        
195|d1a1ab|        for (lineIndex, line) in lines.enumerated() {
196|3a36dc|            for (pattern, type) in patterns {
197|66048b|                if let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern, options: []),
198|0483e7|                   let match = regex.firstMatch(in: line, options: [], range: NSRange(line.startIndex..., in: line)) {
199|dd2193|                    
200|6af780|                    let lastGroupIndex = match.numberOfRanges - 1
201|a2f8cd|                    guard lastGroupIndex > 0,
202|b5e457|                          let range = Range(match.range(at: lastGroupIndex), in: line) else { continue }
203|dd2193|                    
204|134a37|                    let name = String(line[range])
205|dd2193|                    
206|c06721|                    // Skip common keywords
207|98c79c|                    guard !["if", "else", "for", "while", "switch", "catch", "return"].contains(name) else { continue }
208|dd2193|                    
209|62536b|                    symbols.append(CodeSymbol(
210|e8eb2a|                        name: name,
211|dd7229|                        type: type,
212|35d8e4|                        line: lineIndex + 1,
213|6aead8|                        column: 1,
214|56d74d|                        detail: nil,
215|4b2c23|                        containerName: nil
216|c89922|                    ))
217|8dcb2c|                    break
218|4e2d32|                }
219|a7dc16|            }
220|5f3077|        }
221|d6ed84|        
222|1e442a|        return symbols
223|27e597|    }

230|d6ed84|        
231|bc1385|        let patterns: [(pattern: String, type: SymbolType)] = [
232|8fed15|            // Classes
233|f67eee|            (#"^class\s+(\w+)"#, .class),
234|99e881|            // Functions/Methods
235|a3fc2f|            (#"^\s*def\s+(\w+)"#, .function),
236|82cb28|            // Async functions
237|990137|            (#"^\s*async\s+def\s+(\w+)"#, .function),
238|220505|        ]
239|d6ed84|        
240|d1a1ab|        for (lineIndex, line) in lines.enumerated() {
241|3a36dc|            for (pattern, type) in patterns {
242|66048b|                if let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern, options: []),
243|0483e7|                   let match = regex.firstMatch(in: line, options: [], range: NSRange(line.startIndex..., in: line)) {
244|dd2193|                    
245|ed622c|                    guard match.numberOfRanges > 1,
246|874b10|                          let range = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: line) else { continue }
247|dd2193|

249|03b292|                    let symbolType: SymbolType = line.hasPrefix("    ") || line.hasPrefix("\t") ? .method : type
250|dd2193|

255|6aead8|                        column: 1,

258|c89922|                    ))
259|8dcb2c|                    break
260|4e2d32|                }
261|a7dc16|            }
262|5f3077|        }
263|d6ed84|        
264|1e442a|        return symbols
265|27e597|    }

306|cc5fdf|struct GoToSymbolView: View {
307|e5f895|    @ObservedObject var editorCore: EditorCore
308|9417d7|    let onGoToLine: (Int) -> Void
309|b4687f|    
310|d901da|    @State private var searchText = ""
311|6c323c|    @State private var selectedIndex = 0
312|5d18bc|    @State private var symbols: [CodeSymbol] = []
313|983aaf|    @State private var groupByType = false
314|c96b14|    @FocusState private var isSearchFocused: Bool
315|b4687f|    
316|5855fd|    private var filteredSymbols: [CodeSymbol] {
317|93055c|        if searchText.isEmpty {
318|01fcbf|            return symbols
319|5f3077|        }
320|d6ed84|        
321|b7bcfd|        // Check for type filter prefix (e.g., "@:function")
322|17db3e|        if searchText.hasPrefix(":") {
323|bba019|            let typeFilter = String(searchText.dropFirst()).lowercased()
324|2daecd|            return symbols.filter { $0.type.rawValue.lowercased().contains(typeFilter) }
325|5f3077|        }
326|d6ed84|        
327|1e442a|        return symbols
328|da84a0|            .compactMap { symbol -> (CodeSymbol, Int)? in
329|72f225|                guard let score = FuzzyMatcher.score(query: searchText, target: symbol.name) else {
330|024b84|                    return nil
331|4e2d32|                }
332|6aaf70|                return (symbol, score)
333|a7dc16|            }
334|4a2f11|            .sorted { $0.1 > $1.1 }
335|ffcc79|            .map { $0.0 }
336|27e597|    }
337|b4687f|    
338|7b2aba|    private var groupedSymbols: [(SymbolType, [CodeSymbol])] {
339|814219|        let grouped = Dictionary(grouping: filteredSymbols) { $0.type }
340|8dd9fe|        return grouped.sorted { $0.key.rawValue < $1.key.rawValue }
341|27e597|    }

345|27e597|    }

58|1ca737|    private var allFiles: [QuickOpenItem] {
59|6eb9be|        if Self.isUITesting {
60|c8bb21|            return uiTestItems
61|5f3077|        }
62|adc83b|
63|bacef6|        var items: [QuickOpenItem] = []
64|adc83b|

66|9e03c8|        for tab in editorCore.tabs {

69|6ff6d6|                path: tab.url?.deletingLastPathComponent().path ?? "",

84|33c19a|    private func collectFiles(from node: FileTreeNode, items: inout [QuickOpenItem], basePath: String) {
85|6e7ff6|        let currentPath = basePath.isEmpty ? node.name : "\(basePath)/\(node.name)"
86|adc83b|
87|c98b08|        if !node.isDirectory {
88|c6c38f|            // Skip if already in tabs
89|d6cef7|            if !editorCore.tabs.contains(where: { $0.url == node.url }) {
90|919809|                items.append(QuickOpenItem(
91|efd098|                    name: node.name,
92|d63e10|                    path: basePath,
93|fba36c|                    url: node.url,
94|003454|                    isOpen: false,
95|e67d81|                    language: CodeLanguage(from: node.fileExtension)
96|2188d8|                ))
97|a7dc16|            }
98|5f3077|        }
99|adc83b|
100|13b8cd|        for child in node.children {
101|bdd416|            collectFiles(from: child, items: &items, basePath: currentPath)
102|5f3077|        }
103|27e597|    }
104|adc83b|
105|4607f1|    private var filteredFiles: [QuickOpenItem] {
106|93055c|        if searchText.isEmpty {
107|89fbb2|            // Show open files first, then recent
108|064b28|            return allFiles.sorted { a, b in
109|c12ff4|                if a.isOpen && !b.isOpen { return true }
110|4e9d5a|                if !a.isOpen && b.isOpen { return false }
111|daa15c|                return a.name < b.name
112|a7dc16|            }
113|5f3077|        }
114|adc83b|
115|4095c2|        return allFiles
116|b4fa77|            .compactMap { item -> (QuickOpenItem, Int)? in
117|30f548|                // Score against filename and path
118|3d5797|                let nameScore = FuzzyMatcher.score(query: searchText, target: item.name) ?? 0
119|dd9057|                let pathScore = (FuzzyMatcher.score(query: searchText, target: item.fullPath) ?? 0) / 2
120|129579|                let totalScore = max(nameScore, pathScore)
121|adc83b|
122|7f3f4e|                guard totalScore > 0 else { return nil }
123|64a318|                return (item, totalScore)
124|a7dc16|            }
125|4a2f11|            .sorted { $0.1 > $1.1 }
126|ffcc79|            .map { $0.0 }
127|27e597|    }

56|d14e45|        if let index = tabs.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == tab.id }) {
57|dc033d|            tabs.remove(at: index)
58|adc83b|

60|7fb881|            if activeTabId == tab.id {

65|51dd50|                    let newIndex = min(index, tabs.count - 1)
